    "content": "## Video 1:\nChop bacon into small pieces.\nCook the bacon in a pan until crispy, then turn off the heat and let it cool slightly.\nSeparate egg yolks from egg whites and place the yolks in a bowl.\nGrate pecorino romano cheese and add it to the egg yolks.\nAdd freshly ground black pepper to the egg yolk and cheese mixture and mix well.\nBoil water in a pot, add salt, and cook spaghetti until al dente.\nReserve some pasta water before draining the spaghetti.\nAdd a small amount of reserved pasta water to the egg yolk and cheese mixture to help melt the cheese.\nTransfer the cooked spaghetti directly from the pot to the pan with bacon, without draining completely, to retain some pasta water.\nMix the spaghetti with the bacon and then add the egg yolk and cheese mixture, stirring quickly to create a creamy sauce.\nIf needed, add more reserved pasta water to achieve the desired sauce consistency.\nFinish with additional grated pecorino romano cheese and freshly ground black pepper before serving."
  },
  {
    "role": "user",
    "content": "## Video 2:\nCut about half a pound of thick-cut bacon into three-quarter inch pieces.\nHeat a pan over medium heat and add a tiny bit of olive oil.\nAdd the bacon to the pan and slowly render out the fat until the bacon is crispy.\nBoil about four quarts of water and add a tablespoon of kosher salt.\nGrate three ounces each of Pecorino Romano and Parmigiano-Reggiano cheese.\nIn a bowl, whisk together three whole eggs and two egg yolks.\nWhisk the grated cheese into the egg mixture until combined.\nAdd freshly ground black pepper to the egg and cheese mixture to taste.\nOnce the bacon is crispy, remove some for garnish and drain most of the fat, leaving about two tablespoons in the pan.\nCook spaghetti in the boiling water until slightly al dente, about 10 minutes.\nTurn off the heat under the bacon pan and add the cooked spaghetti to the pan.\nAdd the egg and cheese mixture to the spaghetti, stirring gently to coat the pasta without scrambling the eggs.\nIf needed, add a little reserved pasta water to achieve a creamy consistency.\nPlate the pasta and top with additional grated Parmigiano-Reggiano and crispy bacon."
  }

        "type": "text",
        "text": "## Steps:\nGather the ingredients: guanciale (or pancetta), pecorino romano cheese, free-range organic eggs, pasta, black pepper, and optionally garlic.\nBoil water for the pasta, adding a small amount of salt.\nTwist the pasta into the boiling water to prevent sticking and cook for 8 minutes.\nPrepare the guanciale by removing the skin and slicing it into 1 cm thick pieces, then chop into 0.5 cm chunks.\nPlace the guanciale in a cold pan and heat to medium-high to render the fat.\nOptionally, crack a garlic clove and add it to the pan to infuse flavor, then remove it once the guanciale is golden.\nCrack black peppercorns using a pestle and mortar, then sift to use the hotter inner part of the peppercorns.\nCrack eggs into a bowl and add 20 grams of pecorino romano cheese, then whisk together.\nOnce the guanciale is golden and the fat is rendered, turn off the heat.\nTransfer the cooked pasta directly from the water into the pan with guanciale, using some pasta water to stop frying and create an emulsion.\nAdd the egg and cheese mixture to the pasta, tossing and adding more pasta water as needed to create a creamy sauce through emulsification.\nFinish with additional cracked black pepper and a sprinkle of pecorino romano cheese before serving."
